CREATE TABLE S3G_CLN_RCPT_INST_HDR
  (
    RI_LINK_KEY      NUMBER NOT NULL ENABLE,
    COMPANY_ID       NUMBER NOT NULL ENABLE,
    LOCATION_CODE    VARCHAR2(50 BYTE) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    CUSTOMER_ID      NUMBER NOT NULL ENABLE,
    RECEIPT_ID       NUMBER NOT NULL ENABLE,
    INSTALL_RCPT_AMT NUMBER NOT NULL ENABLE,
    CHEQ_RET_ID      NUMBER,
    DOC_STATUS       VARCHAR2(2 BYTE) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    CREATED_BY       NUMBER NOT NULL ENABLE,
    CREATED_ON TIMESTAMP (6) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    MODIFIED_BY NUMBER,
    MODIFIED_ON TIMESTAMP (6),
    RCPT_DTLS_ID NUMBER,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_RCPT_INST_HDR_PK PRIMARY KEY (RI_LINK_KEY) USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645 PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT) TABLESPACE S3GFA ENABLE
  )
  SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING STORAGE
  (
    INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645 PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT
  )
  TABLESPACE S3GFA ;

    MODIFIED_ON TIMESTAMP (6)
  )

  (

  )
  TABLESPACE S3GFA ;

	 MODIFIED_ON  TIMESTAMP (6), 
	 COMPANY_ID  NUMBER
   ) ;

--------------------------------------------------------

  ;
--------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------

  ALTER TABLE  S3G_OR_CUST_CREDIT_LMT  ADD CONSTRAINT  S3G_OR_CUST_CREDIT_LMT_PK  PRIMARY KEY ( CRDT_LMT_ID ) ENABLE;
 
  ALTER TABLE  S3G_OR_CUST_CREDIT_LMT  MODIFY ( CRDT_LMT_ID  NOT NULL ENABLE);

  ALTER TABLE  S3G_OR_CUST_CREDIT_LMT  MODIFY ( CUTOFF_DATE  NOT NULL ENABLE);
 
  ALTER TABLE  S3G_OR_CUST_CREDIT_LMT  MODIFY ( CREATED_BY  NOT NULL ENABLE);

CREATE TABLE FA_EXPN_BOOK_MST
   (	
   EXPN_BOOK_ID NUMBER, 
	EXPN_BOOK_NO VARCHAR2(50 BYTE), 
	COMPANY_ID VARCHAR2(20 BYTE), 
	LOCATION_CODE VARCHAR2(20 BYTE), 
	EXPN_BOOK_DATE TIMESTAMP (6), 
	ENTITY_ID NUMBER, 
	INVOICE_NO VARCHAR2(20 BYTE), 
	INVOICE_DATE TIMESTAMP (6), 
	STATUS VARCHAR2(2 BYTE), 
	REMARKS VARCHAR2(200 BYTE), 
	CREATED_BY VARCHAR2(20 BYTE), 
	CREATED_ON TIMESTAMP (6), 
	MOD_BY NUMBER, 
	MOD_ON VARCHAR2(20 BYTE), 
	DOC_DATE TIMESTAMP (6), 
	TOT_AMOUNT NUMBER(25,4)
   );

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX FA_EXPN_BOOK_MST_PK ON FA_EXPN_BOOK_MST (EXPN_BOOK_ID) 
  PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT);

ALTER TABLE FA_EXPN_BOOK_MST MODIFY (EXPN_BOOK_ID NOT NULL ENABLE);

   (	EXPN_BOOK_DTL_ID NUMBER,

	LPO_DTL_ID NUMBER,

	OTH_VALUE NUMBER(25,4)
   );

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX FA_EXPN_BOOK_DTL_PK ON FA_EXPN_BOOK_DTL (EXPN_BOOK_DTL_ID) 
  PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT);

ALTER TABLE FA_EXPN_BOOK_DTL MODIFY (EXPN_BOOK_DTL_ID NOT NULL ENABLE);

CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_FA_EXPN_BOOK_MST INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 MAXVALUE 99999 MINVALUE 1 NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_FA_EXPN_BOOK_DTL INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 MAXVALUE 99999 MINVALUE 1 NOCACHE;

  CREATE INDEX S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMT_INDEX1 ON  S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMT (ASS_PASAREF_ID, ASSIGNOR_ID, ASSIGNEE_ID, PASAREF_ID,ACC_ASSIGNMENT_ID);
  
--------------------------------------------------------
--  Constraints for Table S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMT
--------------------------------------------------------

  ALTER TABLE S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMT ADD CONSTRAINT S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMT_PK PRIMARY KEY (ACC_ASSIGNMENT_ID);
 
  ALTER TABLE S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMT MODIFY (ACC_ASSIGNMENT_ID NOT NULL ENABLE);
 
  alter table S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMT modify (CREATED_ON not null enable);


--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Table S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMTGURANTOR
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE TABLE S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMTGURANTOR 
   (	
   ACC_ASSIGNMENT_ID NUMBER, 
	GUARANTEE_TYPE_ID NUMBER, 
	GUARANTEE_ID NUMBER,

	CHARGE_SEQUENCE NUMBER
   );
--------------------------------------------------------
--  Constraints for Table S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMTGURANTOR
--------------------------------------------------------

  ALTER TABLE S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMTGURANTOR MODIFY (ACC_ASSIGNMENT_ID NOT NULL ENABLE);
--------------------------------------------------------
--  Ref Constraints for Table S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMTGURANTOR
--------------------------------------------------------

  ALTER TABLE S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMTGURANTOR ADD CONSTRAINT S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMTGURANT_FK1 FOREIGN KEY (ACC_ASSIGNMENT_ID)
	  references S3G_LAD_ACCASSIGNMT (ACC_ASSIGNMENT_ID) enable;

create or replace force view DV_ENTITY_DET (ENTITY_ID, ENTITY_CODE, ENTITY_NAME, ENTITY_TYPE, ENTITY_TYPE_NAME, PROGRAM_ID,ENTITY_TYPE_CODE) as 
  SELECT EM.ENTITY_ID,EM.ENTITY_CODE,EM.ENTITY_NAME,EM.ENTITY_TYPE,EMTYPE.ENTITY_TYPE_NAME,ENTPGM.PROGRAM_ID,EMTYPE.ENTITY_TYPE_CODE FROM S3G_ORG_ENTITYMASTER EM
INNER JOIN S3G_SYSAD_ENTITYTYPE EMTYPE
ON EMTYPE.ENTITY_TYPE_ID=EM.ENTITY_TYPE
INNER JOIN S3G_ORG_ENTITYPROMAP ENTPGM
on ENTPGM.ENTITY_TYPEID=EMTYPE.ENTITY_TYPE_ID;

-----ADDED BY SUSEELA - CODE STATRS TABLE CREATED AND ALTERED ON 07-04-18------

CREATE TABLE S3G_CLN_DCMAST
  (
    DEBTCOLLECTOR_ID   NUMBER(*,0) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    COMPANY_ID         NUMBER(*,0) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    LOB_ID             NUMBER(*,0),
    REGION_ID          NUMBER(*,0),
    LOCATION_CODE      VARCHAR2(30 BYTE),
    DEBTCOLLECTOR_CODE VARCHAR2(25 BYTE) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    EMP_UTPA_ID        NUMBER(*,0),
    DEBTCOLLECTOR_TYPE VARCHAR2(50 BYTE) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    IS_ACTIVE          VARCHAR2(1 BYTE) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    NEXT_LEVEL         NUMBER(*,0),
    SUPER_LEVEL        NUMBER(*,0),
    FREQUENCY_TYPE     NUMBER(*,0),
    CREATED_BY         NUMBER(*,0) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    CREATED_ON TIMESTAMP (6) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    MODIFIED_BY NUMBER(*,0),
    MODIFIED_ON TIMESTAMP (6),
    TXN_ID      NUMBER(*,0),
    LOCATION_ID NUMBER(22,0),
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_DCMAST_PK PRIMARY KEY (DEBTCOLLECTOR_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_DCMAST_S3G_SYSAD__FK1 FOREIGN KEY (LOCATION_ID) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_LOCATIONMASTER (LOCATION_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_DCMAST_S3G_SYSAD__FK2 FOREIGN KEY (COMPANY_ID) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_COMPANYMASTER (COMPANY_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_DCMAST_S3G_SYSAD__FK3 FOREIGN KEY (LOB_ID) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_LOBMASTER (LOB_ID) ENABLE
  ) ;
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER S3G_CLN_DCMAST_TRG BEFORE
  INSERT ON S3G_CLN_DCMAST FOR EACH ROW BEGIN <<COLUMN_SEQUENCES>> BEGIN IF :NEW.DEBTCOLLECTOR_ID IS NULL THEN
  SELECT SEQ_S3G_CLN_DCMAST.NEXTVAL INTO :NEW.DEBTCOLLECTOR_ID FROM DUAL;
END IF;
END COLUMN_SEQUENCES;
END;
/
ALTER TRIGGER S3G_CLN_DCMAST_TRG ENABLE;

CREATE TABLE S3G_AUDIT_HDR
  (
    AUDIT_HDR_ID      NUMBER NOT NULL,
    COMPANY_ID        NUMBER  NOT NULL,
    TABLE_NAME        VARCHAR2(50 BYTE)  NOT NULL,
    DOC_ID            NUMBER  NOT NULL,
    ACTION            CHAR NOT NULL,
    USER_ID           NUMBER NOT NULL,
    ACTION_DATE       DATE NOT NULL,

    CONSTRAINT S3G_AUDIT_HDR_S3G_C_FK1 FOREIGN KEY (COMPANY_ID) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_COMPANYMASTER (COMPANY_ID),
    CONSTRAINT S3G_AUDIT_HDR_S3G_S_FK2 FOREIGN KEY (USER_ID) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_USERMASTER (USER_ID)
  );

  );

CREATE TABLE S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_HDR
  (
    CHQVLT_LNK_KEY NUMBER(22,0) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    COMPANY_ID     NUMBER(22,0),
    LOCATION_ID    NUMBER(22,0),
    PA_SA_REF_ID   NUMBER(22,0),
    CUSTOMER_ID    NUMBER(22,0),
    CREATED_ON DATE,
    CREATED_BY           NUMBER(22,0),
    REASON_FOR_REQ_VAULT VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_H_PK PRIMARY KEY (CHQVLT_LNK_KEY) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_H_FK1 FOREIGN KEY (COMPANY_ID) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_COMPANYMASTER (COMPANY_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_H_FK2 FOREIGN KEY (LOCATION_ID) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_LOCATIONMASTER (LOCATION_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_H_FK3 FOREIGN KEY (PA_SA_REF_ID) REFERENCES S3G_LAD_ACCPASADET (PA_SA_REF_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_H_FK4 FOREIGN KEY (CUSTOMER_ID) REFERENCES S3G_ORG_CUSTMASTER (CUSTOMER_ID) ENABLE,
    Constraint S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_H_FK5 Foreign Key (CREATED_BY) References S3G_SYSAD_USERMASTER (USER_ID) Enable
  ) ;
  
  CREATE TABLE S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_DET
  (
    CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_DET_ID NUMBER NOT NULL ENABLE,
    CHQVLT_LNK_KEY         NUMBER,
    CHQ_NUM                NUMBER(22,0),
    CHQSTATUS              NUMBER(22,0),
    CHQ_DATE               NUMBER(22,0),
    CHQ_AMOUNT             NUMBER(25,4),
    REQUESTED_BY           NUMBER(22,0),
    REQUESTED_DATE DATE,
    REASION     VARCHAR2(500 BYTE),
    DRAWEEBANK  NUMBER(22,0),
    DRAWEEPLACE NUMBER(22,0),
    AUTH_STATUS VARCHAR2(5 BYTE),
    CREATED_ON DATE,
    CREATED_BY     NUMBER(22,0),
    AUTH_USER_ID   NUMBER(22,0),
    INSTALLMENT_NO NUMBER(22,0),
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_D_PK PRIMARY KEY (CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_DET_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_D_FK1 FOREIGN KEY (CHQVLT_LNK_KEY) REFERENCES S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_HDR (CHQVLT_LNK_KEY) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_D_FK2 FOREIGN KEY (REQUESTED_BY) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_USERMASTER (USER_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_D_FK3 FOREIGN KEY (DRAWEEBANK) REFERENCES S3G_CLN_DRAWEEBANKMASTER (DRAWEEBANKMASTER_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_D_FK4 FOREIGN KEY (DRAWEEPLACE) REFERENCES S3G_CLN_DRAWEEBANKBRANCH (DRAWEEBANKBRANCH_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_D_FK5 FOREIGN KEY (CREATED_BY) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_USERMASTER (USER_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_D_FK6 FOREIGN KEY (AUTH_USER_ID) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_USERMASTER (USER_ID) ENABLE
  ) ;
  
  CREATE TABLE S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_SEQ
  (
    SEQ_ID              NUMBER(22,0) NOT NULL ENABLE,
    CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_DET NUMBER(22,0),

    CHQ_HOV_ACK_DATE DATE,
    CHQ_RV_BY NUMBER(22,0),
    CHQ_RV_DATE DATE,

    CHQ_RV_ACK_DATE DATE,
    APPROVED_BY NUMBER(22,0),
    APPROVED_DATE DATE,

    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_S_FK2 FOREIGN KEY (CHQVLT_LNK_KEY) REFERENCES S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_HDR (CHQVLT_LNK_KEY) ENABLE,

    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_S_FK5 FOREIGN KEY (CHQ_HOV_BY) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_USERMASTER (USER_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_S_FK6 FOREIGN KEY (CHQ_HOV_ACK_BY) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_USERMASTER (USER_ID) ENABLE,
    CONSTRAINT S3G_CLN_CHEQUE_RQST_VLT_S_FK7 FOREIGN KEY (CHQ_RV_BY) REFERENCES S3G_SYSAD_USERMASTER (USER_ID) ENABLE,

-- Alter Script Added By  Anbuvel Start

ALTER TABLE TMP_DBT_CRDT_DET ADD LOB_ID NUMBER;
ALTER TABLE TMP_DBT_CRDT_DET ADD BRANCH_ID NUMBER;

merge into S3G_DBT_CRDT_DET  NS 
            Using (SELECT DET.LINK_DNCN_KEY_DET,DET.PA_SA_REF_ID,AC.LOB_ID
FROM S3G_DBT_CRDT_DET DET
INNER JOIN S3G_LAD_ACCPASADET PASA ON PASA.PA_SA_REF_ID=DET.PA_SA_REF_ID
INNER JOIN S3G_LAD_ACCCREATION AC ON AC.ACCOUNT_CREATION_ID=PASA.ACCOUNT_CREATION_ID) TMP
            ON (TMP.LINK_DNCN_KEY_DET=NS.LINK_DNCN_KEY_DET AND TMP.PA_SA_REF_ID=NS.PA_SA_REF_ID)
            when matched then 
              update set NS.LOB_ID =  TMP.LOB_ID;

merge into S3G_DBT_CRDT_DET  NS 
            Using (SELECT DET.LINK_DNCN_KEY_DET,DET.PA_SA_REF_ID,AC.LOCATION_ID
FROM S3G_DBT_CRDT_DET DET
INNER JOIN S3G_LAD_ACCPASADET PASA ON PASA.PA_SA_REF_ID=DET.PA_SA_REF_ID
INNER JOIN S3G_LAD_ACCCREATION AC ON AC.ACCOUNT_CREATION_ID=PASA.ACCOUNT_CREATION_ID) TMP
            ON (TMP.LINK_DNCN_KEY_DET=NS.LINK_DNCN_KEY_DET AND TMP.PA_SA_REF_ID=NS.PA_SA_REF_ID)
            when matched then 
              update set NS.LOCATION_ID =  TMP.LOCATION_ID;
-- Alter Script Added By  Anbuvel End

 CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW DV_S3G_LAD_ACCREPAYSTRUCT (PANUM, INSTALMENT_AMOUNT, PA_SA_REF_ID, LIP_CUST, LIP_COMP, PRINCIPALAMOUNT, FINANCECHARGES,INSTALLMENT_NO) AS 
  SELECT PASA.PANUM,SUM(INSTALLMENTAMOUNT)+NVL(SUM(EXTN.INSTALMENT_AMOUNT),0) AS INSTALLMENTAMOUNT,  PASA.PA_SA_REF_ID,NVL(SUM(EXTN.INSTALMENT_AMOUNT),0) AS  LIP_CUST,
          Nvl(Sum(Extncompany.Instalment_Amount),0) As Lip_Comp,Nvl(Sum(Pasa.Principalamount),0) As Principalamount,Nvl(Sum(Financecharges),0) As Financecharges,PASA.INSTALLMENT_NO
          FROM S3G_LAD_ACCREPAYSTRUCT PASA
          left join S3G_LAD_ACCREPAYSTRUCT_EXTN extn
          on (extn.PA_SA_REF_ID=PASA.PA_SA_REF_ID 
          And Extn.Instalment_No=Pasa.Installment_No And Extn.Cashflow_Flag_Id=108)
          left join S3G_LAD_ACCREPAYSTRUCT_EXTN extnCompany
          On (Extn.Pa_Sa_Ref_Id=Pasa.Pa_Sa_Ref_Id 
          AND EXTN.INSTALMENT_NO=PASA.INSTALLMENT_NO AND EXTN.CASHFLOW_FLAG_ID=109)
          GROUP BY PASA.PA_SA_REF_ID,PASA.PANUM,INSTALLMENT_NO;
